\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00254}00254 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00255}00255 \textcolor{comment}{    Function: gdImageCreateTrueColor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00256}00256 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00257}00257 \textcolor{comment}{      <gdImageCreateTrueColor> is called to create truecolor images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00258}00258 \textcolor{comment}{      with an essentially unlimited number of colors. Invoke}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00259}00259 \textcolor{comment}{      <gdImageCreateTrueColor> with the x and y dimensions of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00260}00260 \textcolor{comment}{      desired image. <gdImageCreateTrueColor> returns a <gdImagePtr>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00261}00261 \textcolor{comment}{      to the new image, or NULL if unable to allocate the image. The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00262}00262 \textcolor{comment}{      image must eventually be destroyed using <gdImageDestroy>().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00263}00263 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00264}00264 \textcolor{comment}{      Truecolor images are always filled with black at creation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l00265}00265 \textcolor{comment}{      time. There is no concept of a "{}background"{} color index.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01158}01158 \textcolor{comment}{/* 2.0.10: before the drawing routines, some code to clip points that are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01159}01159 \textcolor{comment}{ * outside the drawing window.  Nick Atty (nick@canalplan.org.uk)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01160}01160 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01161}01161 \textcolor{comment}{ * This is the Sutherland Hodgman Algorithm, as implemented by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01162}01162 \textcolor{comment}{ * Duvanenko, Robbins and Gyurcsik -\/ SH(DRG) for short.  See Dr Dobb's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01163}01163 \textcolor{comment}{ * Journal, January 1996, pp107-\/110 and 116-\/117}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01164}01164 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01165}01165 \textcolor{comment}{ * Given the end points of a line, and a bounding rectangle (which we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01166}01166 \textcolor{comment}{ * know to be from (0,0) to (SX,SY)), adjust the endpoints to be on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01167}01167 \textcolor{comment}{ * the edges of the rectangle if the line should be drawn at all,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01168}01168 \textcolor{comment}{ * otherwise return a failure code */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01169}01169 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01170}01170 \textcolor{comment}{/* this does "{}one-\/dimensional"{} clipping: note that the second time it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01171}01171 \textcolor{comment}{   is called, all the x parameters refer to height and the y to width}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01172}01172 \textcolor{comment}{   -\/ the comments ignore this (if you can understand it when it's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01173}01173 \textcolor{comment}{   looking at the X parameters, it should become clear what happens on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01174}01174 \textcolor{comment}{   the second call!)  The code is simplified from that in the article,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01175}01175 \textcolor{comment}{   as we know that gd images always start at (0,0) */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{libmscgen_2gd_8c_source_l01176}01176 }
